
 Iziboshwa zothando 

 
'Wena 10 mlungu noma wena 10 Bantu female?' 

  'Ngiyazisa ntombi kaMhlophe. Ngizoke ngizwe namhlanje,' kusho uThandekile ethuswa yizwi lomdlikiza ihlombe. Aphakamise ikhanda amehlo ewasusa emkhiloshweni akade ewenza njengoba ehlezi esitobhini sebhasi esilapha kuChurch Street eMgungundlovu. Amehlo azithela engqansabuleni yengqomondo kanongqayi omhlophe, uSayitsheni Wellem de Wet osemengeme. 
'Hheyi mantombazane, suka!' 

  lyambuka Ie ntokazi, yethuke lapho amehlo ehlangana nakaSayitsheni ansundu, avuthayo. Ithanda nokushiywa yigazi yethuswa nawukungqangqazela kwamadevu ansundu. Nokho isheshe ikwehlise ukwethuka, isimze ithi, 'Yebo, 
I ngiyintombazane, ngingedwa. Angiyena iBantu Female. 
Ngiyisimame, ngingowokudabuka kuleli.' 

  'Mantombazane, wena hhayi yizwa, hhayi bona futhi. Buka,' umkhombisa imicu yobusayitsheni. 'Mina 10 mapoyisa. Zobopha wena' 

  lmhleka usulu intokazi yansondo isimze ithi, 'Mina ngiyintombazane, ngingedwa, nawe uyiphoyisa elilodwa. Uzongibophelani-ke phoyisa?' 

  'Kulesi sihlalo ohlezi kuso kuhlala 10 rna-Europeans kuphela abamhlophe bodwa,' usho abuke ibhasi eli mayo, Iilayishe, lisuke lilibangise ePrestbury. 

  'Nami ngimhlophe nje sithandwa, futhl ngingowakwaMhlophe nangesibongo,' usho eyibuka ngokungayigqizi qakala Ie nsizwa naye azibonelayo ukuthi ivuke yazihlalela ngebrasso izindondo nezinkinobho ezimenyezela eyunifomini. Nezicathulo, yize seziIele uthuli lomgwaqo, kuyacaca ukuthi zike zacwazimulisa okwesibuko. 

  'Yizwa kahle mantombazane. Khipha zigonogono lapha,' emqhafaza indlebe ngeminwe. 'Lo sihlalo kalo mlungu, hhayi kalo Mhlophe. Nasiya 'esikhomba,' 10 sihlalo kalo Non-European usihlalo kamuntu omhlophe njengawe Mhlophe. Wena yenza cala.'

   Aphenduke uSayitsheni, balandeiane babuyele kule nsizwa afike ayijamele athi, 'Kwenzenjani Phineas? Uhlaleleni lapha amfana?' 

  'Nkosana, ubuzelani wazi? Uyazibonela nje nawe ukuthi yithina esisebenza lapha esishayelela izaziso.' 
'Sithini 10 saziso osinyathele?' 

  'Angikwazi min a ukufunda. Ngisinikezwa yinduna, unkosana uMabalengwe. Ngicela ungifundele.' 

Asikhombe isaziso aze asiqongqothe ngendukwana ayiphethe ekhuluma egcizelela ethi, 'Sithi, 10 Europeans kuphela mani; hhayi 10 mllntu!' Umkhomba aze aqhelise ikhanda uPhineas. '0, kanti mina njengoba ngiqongqothela ngingazi nje, ngishayelela ukuthi izihlalo ezabaphesheya kuphela?' 'Awuzwa-ke. Yebo amfana.' 

  'Hhayi-ke, kusengesethu sonke njengoba izaziso zisaxubene phansi nje. Sizoba ngesabaphesheya uma sengiqede iliye lami leli, ngasiqongqothela.' 

  Anikine ikhanda uWellem, abuke uThandekile athi, 'Uyasebenza uPhineas. La ndawo uzoziqedela yena khona 

manje uma esesifakile isaziso. Ngilandele,' edlwayizela emholela kwesifana nabasuke kllSO, sehluke ngesaziso kuphela, nokuthi-ke sona sisodwa vo. 'Wena 10 Non-European, hhayi 10 European. Nangu sihlalo wakho muhle.' 

  'Qha, sihle impela nasa,' emoyizela uThandekile ehlala. 'Ngaphambi kokuba sehlukane, sithandwa, ngizocela nje kesikhumbllzane mhlawumbe ngongakunakile. Konje ubani igama lalo mgwaqo?'

Nokho, kusobala ukuthi Ie ntokazi isiyabejwayela abangamabhoxongwana anjengaye. Ayimkhombisanga ngisho ezincane izimpawu zokwethllka, ukuzwela nokuhluthuka kwenhliziyo. KoPitoli ngahle ukuba base beke baphoxana, bethukana. 
'Uthe ungubani igama lakho mantombazane?'

'Ngicela ungiqashe bandla, nkosana.' Le ntokazi eyipentshisi elisemashumini amabili nesithupha eminyaka, isho ngelimnandi, elincengayo, lihlobe ngalo izinyo elimhiophe. 'Unalo pasi nosipesheli?'

  Nempela bahlale balinganisane engasasibhekanga nokuthi sibhalwe ukuthini. 
  'Mntanabantu, musa ukungihlalisa esihlalweni sabaseYurophu, ungidalele ieala phew kwelinye,' esho emkhombisa umbhalo. 
  'Noma kunjalo, kulungile. Ake sihlale. Ngithanda ukuzwisisa ukuthi ubuthini.' 
  'Ngane yakwethu, bengithi angikutshele nje izinhlamvu zikabhoqo mayelana nokuthi lokhu okwenza kimi nakwabanye angikuthandi, futhi kuphambene namalungelo esintu umhlaba jikelele. Sidalelwe inkululeko, hhayi ukugqilazwa njengoba wenza.' 

  Uyathula uWellem eshaywa amahloni, ebuka noMngwevu omile ethithibele. 
'Lokhu okwenza kithi ungakuthanda na uma kwenziwa kuwe, 

kudadewenu, kumama, kumkakho, kuyihlo nakumfowenu?' UWellem uphendula ngokunikina ikhanda. 
'Pho ukwenzelani kumkakho nakuyihlo?' 
'Hhayi khona mkami lapha. Ntombi yami isePitoli.' 'Ukhona impela umkakho. Yimina 10. Njengoba ungibona 
nje, ubona yen a impela; ubona unyoko; ubona umlamu, ugogo nendodakazi yakho. Uyakuphika lokho?' 
  Wathula manje uWellem amehlo ewathe mbe, phansi. Uze awaphakamise lapho eyizwa iza inyelela, ima ibhasi ephikelele ePrestbury. Ababuke abagibeli begibela, nalapho sebehlezi ngokungehlukani ngezihlalo. Uyadideka. Lisuke linyelele futhi, ziye. 
  'Njengoba usunguSayitsheni nje, nongqayi, kusho khona ukuthi usuvuthiwe engqondweni. Usukuzwile engikushilo. Umake ungase ukuthande ukukuzwa kwenziwa kuwe noma kubahlobo bakho lokhu okwenza kithi, usungasidudulela kule veni yakwenu. Ngizongena kuyo nginesibindi.' 
   'Thandi, ngicela ungakulibali ukuthi wumsebenzi wami 10 engiwenzayo, nesenginqume ukuphila ngawo,' esho ngesiNgisi asephulayo. 
  'lnqobo nje uma uphilela ukwenza ongeke wathanda ukukubona nokukuzwa kwenziwa kuwe, kubahlobo nasohlangeni Iwakini, ngidudulele kumeleko.' 
  Wenwaya ikhanda uWellem, azamule. Uthula isikhathi eside ecweba izinyembezi okungaqondakali ukuthi ngezokuzamula

noma ngezikanembeza yini. Ngesikade athi, 'Angithi Thandi ubuthe ufuna msebenzi?' 
Avume uThandi. 

  '0, kulungile-ke. Mina funa ntombazane ezopheka. Fika kumina kusasa ngemuva kwamadina. Mina hlala lapha Prestbury.' Umbhalela ikheli nenombolo yocingo epheshaneni. Uyalemukela uThandi, alibuke emoyizela qede abuke uWellem, bese ebuza ethi, 'Kunjani kodwa nkosana, kuyahlaleka kwakho, noma nakhona kunezihlalo zabaseYurophu nezabangebona?' 
  'Kulungile, uzobona khona. Kwabafuna umsebenzi, kuyasebenzeka. Kwabafuna inkathazo, amaphekulazikhuni namakhomanisi, baphetha ndaweni ebafanele, ejele,' esemtshela ngolukaJoji. 'Madoda, hamba. Sindela Thandi.' 

  'Ngiyabonga nkosana!' eyishaya eyisheshisa indesheni uMngwevu. 'Nakuwe mntanami ngiyabonga. Ngiyaxolisa.' Ayishaye futhi indesheni, asheshe ahambele phezulu, angaze abizwe ayolala kwabaningi. 
  Behlukaniswa wukufika kwebhasi uThandi aseligibela. Usuka lapho uWellem engasaqhawuzeli. Ngemuva kokuba ibhasi limthathile uThandi lathubeleza naye. kweziningi izimoto, uyalibuka uWellem eliphelezela ngomlozana awushayela ph ansi uzwiwa uye yedwana. 

  'Ukopoletsheni walapha eMgungundlovu oyinkinga kakhulu nosixabanisayo. Ukuba laba bantu bedolobha lalapha akabathwali ngabhasi linye nabamhlophe, ngabe abahlali nakuhlala ezihlalweni zethu njengoba amabhasi aya ezindaweni zabo ngabe ahambeia kude nasesijiwini sedolobha.' Uyancinciza futhi uWellem ebuka elinye ibhasi likakopoletsheni lishushuluza, ezihlalweni kulinganisene izinhlanga ngezinhlanga ezakhele leli. 

  Yebo, ngale nje komphakathi walapha eMgungundlovu' ngokwabo abawubona unamakhanda aqinile, kwakopeletsheni wakhona ubazimukisa amakhanda. Laba bantu uWellem aqikelela ukuthi bahlala emabhentshini ehlukene, ukopeletsheni uyabavumela bagibele bhasi linye nabamhlophe, okuyisenzo esingasenziwa emadolobheni amaningi. 
USayitsheni Wellem de Wet akabe esaq hawuzela emise isifuba. 
Usala enyathela kancane. Uma maqondana nesinye sezihlalo naso esinesaziso. Usibukisisa aze anqekuzise ikhanda efunda 

8 

umbhalo ogqamile obhalwe kuso ngesilungu ukuthi: 'EUROPEANS ONLY'. Eceleni kwawo kunobhalwe ngesiZulu ukuthi, 'ABAMHLOPHE KUPHELA.' UWellem uwubuka kuthi cosololo enhliziyweni, kwehie negwebu inhliziyo elembozwe yizinkulumo zikaThandekile. Uze akhiphe neduku lesandla awusulisise umbhalo othi 'EUROPEANS ONLY'. Kufanele enze kanje. Uneziphandla nezimendlela ezisinda ingalo nje wakhushulwa yikho ukuqikelela ukuthi 10 mthetho uyagcinwa. ENtiiasifali, ePitoli, ushiye eziqondisile izigwegwe zabadukela emabhentshini abaseYurophu. Ulethwe kuleli dolobha nje ngoba kucaca ukuthi baningi uhulumeni athi ebatshela okwakhe bona bebeba amakhanda abatshela akwaba. Umkhakhabisa kabi abekana nesinqe ezihlalweni zabaseYurophu engeyana. Umdansa ngamajazi on gena ngomnyango engabalwa nabo. Amaphikankani uwashadisa nozankosi khona manje. Empeleni njengaba ewuSayitsheni sekufanele ngabe usekhamba kwenziwe ukuba akashiswa yintshisekelo yokunconywa. A, uWellem de Wet!

h. 

2 

Ngomuso, ngehora lesithathu ntambama uThandekile. wehla ebhasini ePrestbury. Nanguya eshaya phansi phezulu nezitaladi efuna inombolo yakwaDe Wet. Wedlula nangesesontweni elidala lasePresbyterian. Ajikajikeleze, agcine eyitholile. Ibude buduze nendlu yesonto lase Presbyterian allzonda kabi uWellem. Linomfundisi ogxeka ingubo kahulumeni. Inombolo ibonakala kahle esangweni lomuzi othe shuthe ngaphansi kwezihlahla. Nokho kuyabonakala ukuthi umuzi usumdala. Ungena esangweni elinesexwayiso ngenja elumayo, aphuthume emnyango enyonyoba, egalaza izinja. Ngenhlanhla yakhe umnyango uvullwe. Ukuthi wumuzi wephoyisa lona awuthandabuzi. Endllni yokuphumula amehlo abingelelwa yiyunlfomu egethuke esihlalweni, ozankosi nezindondo kuwucaca etafuleni. Uhlezi unkosana (njengegama athanda ukubizwa ngalo) komunye wosofa bakwakhe nabo asebebadala, uzidla izindebe ehlikihla izindondo nezinkinobho ngebrasso. 
  Ukunggonggoza kukaThandekile kuyamethusa, athwale amehlo uWellem, kuwe nendondo. Uthi akangene. Nempela uyangena, erne ngasemnyango elindele ukukhonjiswa okungesona esabaseYurophu. Azizwe emangala kuthiwa angahlala kunoma yisiphi asithandayo. Ahiale ngokwesaba. A, kumnandi ukubeka isinge kwesinye sazo nakuba sezibukeka zindadiana nje. Babingelelane baxoxe. 
  Emizuzwini engemingaki engenile uThandekile kuyamcacela ukuthi unkosana 10 wakwaDe Wet obesanda kubitoza waze wafutheka njengeselesele edolobheni, exosha abantu ezihlalweni, ungomunye uWellem uma esekhaya. Emizweni yakhe buyezwakala ubuntu. Ezingxoxweni zabo uchazelwa nokuthi insizwa Ie isicelile, ingoduso yayo uNina Nel isesePitoli Iapho isebenza khona. Bazoshada ezinyangeni ezingengaki, bese ehla bazohlala ndawonye. 

  Bayaphuma akhonjiswe nomuzi. Indlu yalapha ekhaya yesitini esibomvu esingapendiwe. Inamashumi ngamashumi eminyaka yakhiwa. Ifulelwe ngothayeia opendwe ngopende

osasiliva. Nakuba ngaphambi kwendlu igceke lilincane, nokho IItshalwe nongwengwe oluhlobe ngezimbali. Ukhonjiswa nezindlu zezisebenzi ezibizwa ngeyomfana neyentombazane . 
. Ziyizindlwana ezingemuva kwendlu enkulu. Zithe gekelele ngemuvana kwegaraji nalo ellngemuva. Zingohhafudakana abalinganisene bephahle indlu yangasese. Zombili azikangeni muntu njengoba uWellem ezibika ukuba mandlamafishane, ekhala ngomholo athi awukamvumeli ukuba agashe ambiza ngelomfana wezivande. 
Indlu evulwayo kuthiwa izohlala uThandekile. Incane. 
Inezindonga ezazike zaluhlaza. Seziphushelwe wupende. 
Yilokhu okuyenza idangale, idikibale. Inombhede wensimbi omilenze midekazi ebukeka ilidinga impela iladi. Eceleni kwawo kunekhabeshana elincane. Odongeni kuncike iwadirobhu esindala. Ighumile engxenye. Ezansi ngasemnyango kunetafudlana elinamasosipani amnyama, amapani anjalo nawo, nephulamastofu endala, engcolile. Phinde, lapha endlini ayikho ipulaki kagesi. Okukhona mayelana nogesi yizinkinobho zokukhanyisa ugesi wangaphandle nowasendlini. Nogesi ophezulu sewalala uthull nolwembu. Ukhanyisa okwesiphefu somele upharafini. 
  'Yilona kamelo lakho-ke leli mantombazane. Uzohlala ukhululeke. Lilungise-ke bese ulanda mpahla yakho ukuze ugale kusebenza ngomuso.' 
Abonge uThandekile, bese ecela iyunifomu. 'Landela mina mantombazane.' 
  Nempela uThandekile amlandele, bangene endlini lapho uWellem esithela khona kwelinye ikamelo. Dukuduku abuye nayo iyunifomu yasemajalidini. Eyibuka nje, yinkulu kunaye. Umjikijelela yona, ayemukela abonge. Kuba ukugala kwakhe ukuhlanza indlu, ajuluke abe manzi nte. Isiyome kege, unikwa nemall yokulanda izimpahla. Angene indlela, ahambe aze abuye ngokuhlwa. 
  Kuba ukumazisa nje uWellem ukuthi usebuyile, uThandekile wansondo azivalele, avule imigingo yakhe afunde. Ulala kwamabili, ala Ie sinye. Uvuka kusa eseyolungisela uWellem amnggonggozela amthole esevukile, waggoka. Adidizele emlungisela isikhafu.

  Akakazi phela ukuthi emazingeni aphezulu kwezombusazwe akusalalwa, kudingidwa lona udaba ngalawa magama. Uthando lukaHarris noNobuhle, uWellem noThandekile, luyenzile 
indaba. Nempela iziphathimandla zigeina zinqume ukuba esulwe amagama amadala, kuqoshwe amasha. 
  Ngemuva kwalokho abuthiwa quthu ubuthongo, kuqoshwa othayela abasha. Leyo mibhalo ezoshesha ukutholakala kufanele iqale ngokufakwa khona eMgungundlovu ukuze 
- uKopeletsheni, abantu bakhona noWellem asebemthumbile, bagotshwe inkani kusashisa nje. Nempela amaloli 

akwahulumeni ayatheleka nemibhalo eyizintaba ngezintaba ezisemabhokisi. nizongazi. Angiyona mina into yokudlala. NgiwuKheneli Piet Graves.' Adonse iphephandaba lesilungu eliseduze kwakhe. Umbiko obhalwe ngamagama amakhulu kulo uwufunda ahleke kakhulu enqekuzisa ikhada. Uthi: 'UMKHANDLU-DOLOBHA WASEMGUNGUNDLOVU UWASHAYA INDALI AMABHASI AWO'. 
  Kusenjalo kukhale ucingo. Alubambe. Luphuma entokazini eyamukela abeze lapha emahhovisi. Ithi u]enene de Wet ohambisana nomunye ucela ukumbona njengoba ubevele ebekise lesi sikhathi ngocingo. Athi abamlethe. Dukuduku angene. kwile inhliziyo kaGraves lapho embona engena, elandelwa wuHennie Malherbe. Bahlale ezihlalweni, baqale ngokuzixoxela ezimthokozisayo uPiet, zokudayiswa kwamabhasi akwaMasipala. 
  'Njengoba ungibona nje Piet ngilapha, ngilethwa yindumalo,' kusho u]enene de Wet obonakala ngisho ebusweni ukuthi udumele. 
  'Udumele ngakhona ]enene. Akudlali ukuzala insizwa yakho enhle kanje, uyizalela ukuba idunyiswe ikhanda ngabantu besimame abamnyama.'

  Phezu kokuba kunje, uyaqhubeka umcimbi phansi emgwaqweni laphaya. Iza kancane enye ibhasi. Iyema. Bayagibela abagibeli asebekade behlezi belingasene zihlalweni zinye. Sebehlala ndawonye. Yasuka yanyelela, kwavela izandla emafasiteleni bethathazelana neMeya noMkhandlu-dolobha wabo, nezihlwele eziphansi. Yahamba yaze yayosithela, abanye beYlthela ngezmyembezi zenjabulo nezenkumbulo. 
  Alunguze ephezulu uKheneli Piet Graves, azikhalele ethi 'Yeka ukuba amandla ami bengiwasebenzisela ubunye kunonya?' Edldeklle, esefana nohlanya, amemeze, aphakamise isandla

ethi,'Meya! Meya! Uxolo mfowethu! Halala mntakamama ngokusheshe ukhanyiselwe ngenkambo yeqlniso!' Athathe izipopolo futhi abuke phansi, bese ememeza ethi, 'Meya mntakamama!' eqhweba ngesinye isandla, 'misa leyo bhasi. Nami ngifuna ukugibela nalabo ngiyohlambuluka, ngizixolisele kuMvelinqangi ngisesontweni ePrestbury!' 
  'Halala kuwe Mvelinqangi! Halala Meya nomkhandlul Halala Mgungundlovu!' NoDe Wet noMalherbe besho bephakamisa izandla, behalalisa kanye kanye sengathi batshelene. 
  'Ukuthula nothando kubantu emhlabeni, nodumo malube kuMvelinqangi kunaseziphathimandleni zasemhlabeni nezikhundla zalO!' esesho yedwa u]enene de Wet, esiphakamisa isandla, qede esifinyeza, ekhothama. 
  'Uyobuya nini kodwa mntanami engakugcweleza, ngizixolisele kuwe ngingakafi?' ehhema uPiet. 
  'Xolisa Piet esizweni nasemhlabeni ngokuqala manje ukusebenzela ukulunga, wenze nanjengoba asithuma umntanami, uWeIlem de Wet,' kusho uHennie esaliphethe iBhayibheli alithatha kuBoshoff. Ubabuka abadabukele. Uyazi uzoke ehlukane nabo isikhathi eside. Usehlelile nezinhlangano lOmzabalalO. Naye uyeqa ngomuso, uyosebenzisana noWeIlem. 
  Lihamba impela ibhasi. Nantiya, nezandla zabathathazelayo zilokhu zivele njalo emafasiteleni. Lilibangisephi kodwa bakithi? Liya khona impela ePrestbury, ngaseMayors Walk. Liqhamukela ePrestbury qede zikhale izinsimbi zesonto.
